*************************************************************************************
The KnownDLLs subkey defines the set of dynamic-link libraries (DLLs) that are searched during system startup.
In general, these are system DLLs that are loaded from disk into a section of memory and are then checked for integrity.
 These DLLs consume some resources, even if no application loads them.
